About Pincode 421002

PIN code 421002 consisits of 6 digit code which is used to find out post offices in district in India. The first digit of a PIN indicates the zone (Northern/ Western/ Southern/ Eestern). For the pincode 421002, first digit is "4" so zone is Western. The second digit indicates the sub-zone. Here combination of first two digit is "42" So this denotes to the state Maharashtra, and the third, combined with the first two, indicates the sorting district within that zone. The final three digits are assigned to individual post offices within the sorting district.
